style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">敏捷，试图消除的是“需求变更”和“交付周期”中的等待与返工的浪费；DevOps，试图消除的是“开发”与“运维”两个孤岛之间，因流程、工具不统一而产生的部署和协作的浪费。这些理论的本质，是为了解决一个根本性问题：软件开发是团队协作的产物，而只要有协作，就必然有沟通、等待、交接所带来的摩擦和损耗。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">如果一个项目从头到尾都由一个人完成，他就不需要敏捷，也不需要 DevOps，因为不存在协作的浪费。但现实是，任何有一定规模的软件都离不开团队。因此，传统研发效能的核心，就是不断优化“人与人”之间的协作流程，以求消除浪费。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">那么，AI 时代呢？生产力工具的爆炸式提升，是否意味着这个核心逻辑就变了？</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">笔者认为，恰恰相反，这个核心逻辑不仅没有变，反而被前所未有地凸显和放大了。 只是，我们需要消除的浪费，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">除了传统的“人与人”之间，又增加了一个全新的、也可能是未来最大的浪费来源：人与AI之间的协作浪费。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">AI 有哪些浪费</span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">又</span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">可能</span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">如何消除</span></span></h3><h3 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:14pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></h3><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">对于未来具体会演变成什么样的新流程，笔者不敢断言，毕竟实践是检验真理的唯一标准。</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">过去我们总结敏捷、DevOps 等范式，也是基于业界无数团队长达数年的实践和沉淀。如今AI才刚刚起步，谈论一个成熟的“AI Native研发流程”还为时尚早。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">但这并不妨碍我们基于自己的实践，去窥视和随想一番。根据笔者这两年在各种项目中与AI“并肩作战”的经历，确实观察到了一些新的、非常具体的“浪费”正在浮现。未来的新流程</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">可能</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">是围绕着</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">类似</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">浪费而展开。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">比如，最直观的一种浪费，就是我们花费在解释上的时间。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">在一个大型项目中，代码结构复杂，业务逻辑盘根错节。你可能需要先花上几分钟，像老师教学生一样，耐心地向AI解释当前这个模块的架构、核心数据流、以及你接下来想做什么。一通解释下来，AI总算“听懂了”，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">能</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">开始帮你干活。但如果你临时切换到另一个不相关的Bug修复，再切回来时，很抱歉，它的“短期记忆”已经清空，你又得把刚才那番话再对它讲一遍。这种上下文反复建立的浪费，在笔者看来，是当前人机协作效率的最大瓶颈之一。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这种</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">情况</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">笔者</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">目前</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">采取</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">策略</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">是</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">定期把</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">重要</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">逻辑流程作为</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">一个</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">基础文档， 有了 AI ，笔者写文档的数量越来越多，因为文档是最简洁的代码抽象。 但</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这样</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">还</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">不够</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">为了</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">准确</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">还原</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">出</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">仓库</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">因</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">提示词</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">版本</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">而</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">变更</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">记录</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">笔者</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">还会</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">建立</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">一个</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">prompts&nbsp;as&nbsp;code</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""></span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""></span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">提示词</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">代码</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">文档。未来，有</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">机会</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">再</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">深入</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">分享这些</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">AI</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">编程</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">的</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">经验。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">与之相关的，是另一种大多数 AI 使用者可能遇到过，想要砸键盘的浪费，笔者称之为</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">能力边界的误判</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这种误判有两个极端。一个极端是低估了它，有时候你吭哧吭哧花半天时间手写一个复杂的函数，写完了一测试，发现各种边界Case没考虑到。抱着试试看的心态问了一下AI，结果它一分钟就给出了一个更健壮、更优雅的实现。这半天的功夫，浪费得让人扼腕。另一个极端则是高估了它，也是笔者大多情况遇到的，你满怀信心地让AI去实现一个包含复杂状态机的业务逻辑，结果它反复出错，给出的代码漏洞百出，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">你陪着它“调试”了半天，最后发现还不如自己从头写来得快。这种因为不了解AI能力边界而导致的大量无效尝试，也是一种巨大的隐性浪费。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">当然，还有我们最容易想到的，在各种工具之间来回切换的浪费。一会儿在IDE里写代码，一会儿切到ChatGPT的网页窗口问问题</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">未来</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">可能</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">会</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">有</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">大量内部&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">AI</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">工具</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">，</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">信息在不同窗口之间割裂，思路也频繁被打断</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">笔者主要从开发的视角观察，但可以想见，这些新的浪费绝不只存在于编码环节。一个产品经理，要如何高效地向AI描述一个复杂的用户场景，才能得到一份像样的PRD草稿？一个测试工程师，要如何判断哪些测试用例可以放心交给AI生成，哪些又必须亲力亲为地设计？</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">这些问题，本质上都是一样的，都是在探索人与AI协作的最优路径，消除其中的种种浪费。</span></span></p><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf=""><br></span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><h2 style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">结</span></span><span style="font-size:16pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;"><o:p></o:p></span></h2><p style="text-align:justify;margin-top:3pt;margin-bottom:3pt;margin-left:0pt;margin-right:0pt;"><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">未来的研发流程，或许不会再有像“敏捷”或“DevOps”这样宏大而统一的范式。它可能会变得更加“因地制宜”，更加依赖于团队成员与AI的磨合程度。</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">现在</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">范式</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">过程</span></span><span 巨头</span></span><span style="font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang SC;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#333333;letter-spacing:0pt;mso-font-width:100%;vertical-align:baseline;" ><span leaf="">布局</span></span><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:PingFang
